name:Gâ€Lâ€9â€5â€1â€1â€9
info:Executive Double Room
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Solo travelers
info:24 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted May 4, 2024
msg:This time I stayed on the executive floor. Let me first say the good things. The room facilities are quite satisfactory. They have all the facilities that should be available at this level, and the sound insulation is good. The service is warm and fast. The view outside the room window is nice. There are welcome fruits on the first day, and there are free soft drinks in the minbar. The breakfast is good, with regional characteristics. Chicken soup fried rice, pancakes, and beef patties are recommended. There are not many people in the swimming pool, and the management is basically in place.
Then let's talk about the problems. First, the room temperature is too high. It is more than ten degrees outside and 27 degrees in the room. The hotel started the central air conditioning at night on the first night, and the temperature dropped to 24, which was quite comfortable. On the second night, the front desk said that the outdoor temperature was low and the cooling could not be turned on. Then the room was always 27 degrees. . . . . Although they sent an electric fan and helped to open the window, it was not very useful. I didn't sleep well all night. It really needs to be improved! ! Whether the central air conditioning is turned on or not depends on the indoor temperature. Second, the min bar refrigerator is transparent glass, with a light inside, which is always on. The light is very obvious at night, brighter than the night light. It needs to be optimized, at least the light can be turned off. Third, light stains can be seen on light-colored carpets. I asked the cleaning staff to do a secondary trea**ent, but the effect was not obvious. Light-colored carpets still need regular deep cleaning.
